3. When bondholders apply for added interest coupons or exchange for new bonds, they should obtain an application form from the managing agency, fill it out according to the format, and specify the type, number of bonds, and denomination, as well as attach the number of unmatured interest coupons or principal and interest coupons. On the front of the original bond, to the right of the Ministry of Finance seal, each bond should be stamped with the applicant's personal seal or signature, and the application form should also be stamped with the same seal or signature. Those applying for added interest coupons should stamp or sign the upper left corner of the bond for Military Expenditure Bonds, the lower right corner for Disbandment Bonds, the upper right corner for 19th Year Customs Bonds, and the lower right corner for 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds and 20th Year Financial Bonds, and transcribe the original bond number in the blank space. All should be submitted to the Bond Exchange Office or the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations to obtain a temporary receipt. 4. When the Bond Exchange Office or the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications receive the aforementioned application form and bonds, they should first verify whether the number of bonds and attached interest coupons or principal and interest coupons matches the information provided in the application form. Next, they should verify whether the bond and application form have been stamped with the applicant's personal seal or signature. If applying for added interest coupons, they must also verify that the number copied on the corner to be cut off is correct and that it has been stamped or signed with the same seal or signature, and verify that the original bond number has not been drawn for redemption. If it has been drawn, it should be immediately returned to the bondholder, and they should be informed to take it to the managing bank to redeem the principal. After verifying that the received bonds are correct, a temporary receipt should be issued and given to the bondholder for safekeeping. 5. For the aforementioned temporary receipt, the Bond Exchange Office will use a two-part form, with one part for the stub and one part for the bondholder. The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications will use a four-part form, with the first part as the receipt, the second part as the notification slip, the third part as the report form, and the fourth part as the stub. The aforementioned four-part receipt will be printed in red by the Central Bank of China, in blue by the Bank of China, and in green by the Bank of Communications. Each managing bank will print them themselves, but the format, paper size, and colors must all conform to the model issued by the Ministry. 6. The following interest coupons and principal and interest coupons should be submitted for the aforementioned six types of bonds: Six interest coupons from No. 16 to No. 21 for Military Expenditure Bonds; six interest coupons from No. 15 to No. 20 for Disbandment Bonds; eight interest coupons from No. 13 to No. 20 for 19th Year Customs Bonds; eleven interest coupons from No. 10 to No. 20 for 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds; seven interest coupons from No. 9 to No. 15 for 20th Year Financial Bonds; and twenty-seven principal and interest coupons from No. 40 to No. 66 for 19th Year Post-Reorganization Treasury Bills. If any of the aforementioned attached interest coupons or principal and interest coupons are missing, the Bond Exchange Office should deduct the missing number of periods and coupons from the added interest coupons or new bonds to be issued, and provide a voucher to the bondholder for safekeeping. If the exchange is handled on behalf of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, or the Bank of Communications, the Bond Exchange Office will hand over this voucher to the three banks for forwarding. 7. If the aforementioned missing interest coupons or principal and interest coupons are later found, the bondholder may, together with the original voucher, take them to the Bond Exchange Office or entrust them to the managing bank to exchange for the previously deducted new interest coupons or principal and interest coupons. However, if the interest coupons or principal and interest coupons are found after the three-year redemption period has expired, or if the voucher is lost when they are found, they will be deemed invalid, and the previously deducted new interest coupons or principal and interest coupons cannot be reclaimed. The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications should pay special attention to the bondholders' missing interest coupons or principal and interest coupons, and clearly indicate them on the temporary receipt, notification slip, report form, and stub. The Bond Exchange Office should properly preserve the aforementioned deducted new interest coupons or principal and interest coupons for bondholders to claim at any time, and report a list of them to the Ministry of Finance on a ten-day basis for record-keeping. 8. The Bond Exchange Office or the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations should examine the secret marks, cross-check the numbers, and the attached interest coupons or principal and interest coupons of the bonds received each day. After verifying that they are correct, for those applying for added interest coupons, the bonds should be temporarily preserved. For Military Expenditure Bonds, a rectangular corner of nine centimeters vertically and six centimeters horizontally should be cut off from the upper left corner of the front of the bond. For Disbandment Bonds, a corner should be cut off from the lower right corner. For 19th Year Customs Bonds, a corner should be cut off from the upper right corner. For 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds and 20th Year Financial Bonds, a corner should be cut off from the lower right corner. For 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds, the corner should be six centimeters vertically and nine centimeters horizontally, and for 20th Year Financial Bonds, the corner should be six centimeters vertically and twelve centimeters horizontally. The seal of the managing agency should be stamped on the corner (corner size as shown in the diagram on the left). On the bond, a stamp should be added indicating that the added interest coupons have been issued from number X to number Y. For the 19th Year Post-Reorganization Treasury Bills, a cancellation stamp should be added to the center of the front of the bond, and the stamp should conform to the Ministry's prescribed format.

9. The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications should deliver the corners of Military Expenditure Bonds, Disbandment Bonds, 19th Year Customs Bonds, 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds, and 20th Year Financial Bonds, or the old 19th Year Post-Reorganization Treasury Bills, along with the notification slips for applying for added interest coupons or exchanging for new bonds, sent from their branches in various locations, to the Bond Exchange Office to obtain a receipt. 10. After receiving the bond corners or old bills delivered by the bondholders or the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, the Bond Exchange Office should, within five days, after verifying that they are correct, issue the added interest coupons or new bills based on the temporary receipt or receipt. If the number of items submitted is excessive and the verification cannot be completed on schedule, the exchange period may be extended. 11. The Bond Exchange Office should issue all added interest coupons or new bonds according to the denomination of the corners or old bills submitted, but the denominations of large and small bills may be adjusted as appropriate. If bondholders require large or small bills for the 19th Year Post-Reorganization Treasury Bills, they may state so when applying for the exchange and pay a printing fee of 1.25 per mille according to the denomination of the type of bill specified, which will also be handled accordingly. If the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications collect this printing fee on behalf, they should submit it along with the old bills to the Bond Exchange Office for verification and receipt. 12. Bondholders may, after five days, stamp the back of the temporary receipt with the same seal or signature as on the application form and take it to the Bond Exchange Office to collect the added interest coupons and the original bonds, or exchange for new bonds. Those who entrust the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications to collect on their behalf may collect from the original managing bank on the agreed date, the date being determined by the managing bank in consideration of the distance of the journey. 13. The Ministry of Finance entrusts the Central Bank to keep the aforementioned added interest coupons and new bonds prepared for issuance, and the Bond Exchange Office may apply for them from time to time for exchange. 14. The Bond Exchange Office should punch holes in all the received bond corners or old bonds, taking care not to damage the seal or signature of the bondholder and the number on the bond, and should classify them by type, compile them into bundles of fifty, and send them to the National Debt Fund Management Committee for safekeeping, pending destruction, and submit a list along with the exchange situation to the Ministry of Finance on a ten-day basis for record-keeping. 15. When the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications in various locations send out the bond corners or old bonds, they should immediately fill out and send a mailing or transportation report form to the head office for forwarding to the Ministry of Finance for record-keeping. The format of the report form is the same as the form for reporting the payment of interest coupons by mail or transportation. The Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications also apply the aforementioned report form when mailing or transporting added interest coupons or new bonds, fill it out and report it to the Ministry for record-keeping, but must add the words "added interest coupons" or "new bonds" to indicate the distinction. 16. The added interest coupons for Military Expenditure Bonds will begin to be issued on January 29th of the 23rd year of the Republic and will end on January 28th of the 24th year. The added interest coupons for the 19th Year Customs Bonds will begin to be issued on February 24th of the 23rd year of the Republic and will end on February 23rd of the 24th year. The added interest coupons for Disbandment Bonds will begin to be issued on March 10th of the 23rd year of the Republic and will end on March 9th of the 24th year. The added interest coupons for 20th Year Financial Bonds will begin to be issued on March 24th of the 23rd year of the Republic and will end on March 23rd of the 24th year. The added interest coupons for 20th Year Disaster Relief Bonds will begin to be issued on April 5th of the 23rd year of the Republic and will end on April 4th of the 24th year. The exchange of new bonds for the 19th Year Post-Reorganization Treasury Bills will begin on February 10th of the 23rd year of the Republic and will end on February 9th of the 24th year.

Current Commentary

Trends in European Politics 3

Shu

丨After the Meeting Between Simon and Mussolini丨

British Foreign Secretary Simon met with Blackshirt Prime Minister Mussolini in Rome. What exactly was discussed and whether a concrete agreement was reached remains to be seen. From the perspective of time and reason, it is unlikely that things could move so quickly. However, the Italian Prime Minister's opinions are biased towards artificial changes to the League of Nations and technical issues regarding arms reduction. Italy already announced its intention to reorganize the League of Nations at the end of last year. On the surface, this seems to fully sympathize with Germany's movement to revise the Treaty of Versailles and is in clear opposition to France. In reality, Italy wants to use Germany's strength to control France and use the reorganization of the League of Nations to change the current organization where small countries have the same voting rights as large countries in League of Nations meetings. This would reduce France's manipulation in Central Europe and increase Italy's possibility of achieving hegemony. This kind of move is enough to arouse some sympathy from Germany. However, on the other hand, it will provoke the resentment of the small countries in Central Europe. Because they are led by France, they can indirectly obtain some benefits due to their opposition to Germany. They also have room to speak and deliberate at League of Nations meetings. If Italy's proposal is implemented, the vested rights of small countries will inevitably be deprived. After the excessive development of nationalism, the survival of small countries is particularly worrying. Therefore, the Little Entente will become increasingly dependent on France, and Poland's opposition to Germany will become more serious. Therefore, I say that Italy's desire to reorganize the League of Nations is ultimately just a one-sided ideal.

As for changing Article 16 of the Covenant to revise the provisions on the inviolability of national territory and ensuring that the League of Nations Covenant is practically implementable, this fundamentally denies the League of Nations and repeats international disputes, exacerbating the stalemate in Europe and even the world. The League of Nations has always held high the banner of pacifism and international cooperation. In fact, all countries in the world, whether economically or politically, are moving towards isolationism, such as economic alliances, increasing tariffs, strengthening armaments, building warships, and promoting military-industrial production. All these facts show that they are preparing for war. However, except for Japan, the major countries are all maintaining a peaceful state and are not willing to take risks lightly in the use of force. Therefore, this League of Nations, which only has a semblance of substance, still has a slight influence in the diplomatic arena. If this kind of provision that only has moral scope is also removed, I am afraid that ambitious countries will become more barbaric and have no limits.

Regarding the issue of arms reduction, observing the world as a whole, it seems that countries have abandoned the peace movement in the past year and turned to arms competition. In capitalist countries, most are strengthening their military and making their existing troops more powerful. Even the socialist Soviet Union is working hard to strengthen its national defense, mechanize its army, and prepare for national mobilization, even surpassing Japan. Therefore, the so-called arms reduction is at most a temporary respite to avoid the current economic panic. The current situation in Europe, with the conflict between Germany and France, is most likely to lead to direct conflict. This is why it is necessary to seek a way to ease the situation.

The so-called crisis of 1936 did not originate in Europe. Because the Washington Naval Treaty is expiring, the three major naval powers, based on the current situation, find it difficult to continue the 5:5:3 ratio. Japan's demand for equality is even more difficult for Britain and the United States to accept. It is recognized that hegemony over the Pacific Ocean, especially in the Western Pacific, has been seized by Japan. In order to develop future markets and maintain the current situation, the United States has no choice but to expand its existing naval power. Japan will naturally catch up quickly, and Britain will not be left behind. Thus, the naval race begins, and the crisis becomes more apparent. However, Japan's national strength is limited. Although modern industry has developed considerably, natural resources are weak. Economic development is difficult to achieve in a short period of time. Therefore, Japanese Foreign Minister Hirota has reset the diplomatic policy, creating a smokescreen of Japanese military action in an attempt to delay military competition and escape its international isolation. However, this makes the League of Nations' position more difficult, and the term arms reduction may in fact be counterproductive.

League of Nations Technical Cooperation Expert Choutens Arrives in Peiping 4

Will Go to Nanking after a Two-Week Stay

(Peiping) League of Nations technical cooperation expert Choutens (French), left Belgium last August to go to Mexico to attend the 22nd League of Nations Statistical Conference. Then, he went to America to give lectures on international cooperation issues. He left America on December 10th to go to Japan, and arrived in China from Japan on the 28th. He arrived in Peiping on the evening of the 4th and is scheduled to stay for two weeks, then he will go to Nanking to visit our government authorities. On the 8th and 9th, at the invitation of the Sino-French University and Peking University, he will give lectures on [the possibility of realizing international cooperation]. According to Choutens, he has assisted more than 40 international organizations and the governments of 12 countries with technical problems, but no government or organization has had long-term work, especially in League of Nations work. He has also practically participated in international cooperation with the League of Nations Labor Bureau in Geneva and is very interested. This time he is traveling around the world, hoping that countries can achieve closer cooperation. In the past 15 years, I have only assisted various international conferences, such as administrative, diplomatic, political, and technical, etc., and have not made much contribution. The League of Nations is deeply dissatisfied with Japan's occupation of the Northeast. China is currently facing serious difficulties, and due to the constraints of various unequal treaties, it is unable to cooperate effectively with the League of Nations, which is very regrettable. In the future, he will work hard to promote its progress. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 5th)

North China War Zone Relief Committee Holds Plenary Session Yesterday 5

(Peiping) The North China War Zone Relief Committee held a plenary session at 10 a.m. on the 5th. Huang Fu, Yu Xuezhong, Song Zheyuan, Wang Kemin, Li Yuanshan, Zhang Boling, Tang Erhe, Wang Yitang, Jiang Menglin, Zhou Yichun, Bian Baimei, Tao Menghe, Li Qin, and He Qigong attended, and Yin Rugeng, Tao Shangming, and Xia Qingyi were present as observers. The following matters were discussed: (1) The Agricultural Relief Group proposed that mutual aid societies in various counties have been established one after another, and requested that relief funds be allocated according to the proposal. It was resolved to allocate the funds to the Financial Group according to the proposal after the government bonds are pledged. (2) The Emergency Relief Group submitted a work relief plan and requested that it be decided upon. It was resolved to first plan within the scope of 700,000 yuan and hand it over to the Emergency Relief Group for replanning, and the Standing Committee will review and handle it. (3) Yin Rugeng, the commissioner of the Jizhou-Miyun District, suggested that long-distance telephones in various counties in the war zone should be repaired to facilitate transportation, and requested a public decision. It was resolved to include it in the work relief plan and handle it together. (4) The Chahar Provincial Government requested the allocation of relief funds. It was resolved to temporarily allocate 100,000 yuan according to the resolution of the fourth meeting of the Political and Rectification Council. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 5th)

Feng Zhanhai's Subordinate, Regiment Commander Xing Yuchou, Goes Missing After Being Detained 6

(Peiping) Xing Yuchou, the detained regiment commander of Feng Zhanhai's subordinate unit stationed in Huailai, went missing on the 4th. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

Hebei Province Strictly Prohibits Opium 7

(Tianjin) Wei Jian, the Director of Civil Affairs, said that starting from New Year's Day, the entire province will strictly prohibit opium. Opium addiction treatment centers will be established in various counties to order opium addicts to register and quit opium within a time limit. Punishments for civil servants who smoke opium will also be stipulated, and it is planned to completely eliminate the three aspects of transportation, planting, and smoking within six months. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

Hunan Provincial Government Passes Loan Contract for Road Construction 8

(Changsha) The Provincial Government passed a contract on the 5th to borrow 200,000 yuan from a banking group to build roads, to be repaid in six months with a monthly interest rate of one percent. The machinery factories will be merged, and Liu Yuehou will concurrently serve as the director of the Highway Bureau and the factories. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

Situation in Xinjiang Province Eases 9

Central Government Organizes Rehabilitation Committee

(Nanking) According to reliable sources, after the turmoil in Xinjiang, Dihua is indeed in the hands of the provincial authorities. Liu Wenlong and Sheng Shicai jointly telegraphed Nanking yesterday to send New Year's greetings to the ministers of various departments. Ma Zhongying and Zhang Peiyuan are jointly opposing Sheng, and the situation is gradually easing. The fighting seems to have stopped. The central government has organized a rehabilitation committee, which will be established soon to start handling the rehabilitation of Xinjiang Province and find ways to develop it. (Central News Agency Dispatch, 5th)

Han Fuju Will Visit Qingdao 10

(Qingdao) Han Fuju is scheduled to come to Qingdao by armored train from Jinan at 8:00 p.m. on the 6th. Ge Guangting will travel with him. Shen Honglie said that Han came for sightseeing and there were no official matters to discuss. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

Shandong Construction Department Decides to Dredge the Rivers in Western Shandong 11

Requests Approval for Provincial Funds to Establish a Domestic Goods Business Firm

(Jinan) The Construction Department has decided to dredge all the rivers in western Shandong starting from March. It has also requested approval for 20,000 yuan in provincial funds to establish a domestic goods business firm to wholesale domestic goods to various counties. The Shanghai domestic goods industry has decided to jointly come to Jinan to establish a domestic goods company, and another group will specialize in wholesale. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

(Jinan) The Jinan Japanese Consular Service Department visited Zhang Honglie, Director of the Construction Department, today to inquire about the government's order to reorganize the Boshan coal mining industry into a joint production and sales company and what its purpose was. Zhang replied that it was to improve foreign credit, such as the Luda Company jointly run by China and Japan, which is considered beneficial and can also be joined. The Construction Department and the Bank of China, the China Cotton Industry Association, and the Liji Flower Shop have also signed ten cooperation measures to promote the cotton industry in the province, first establishing cotton ginning factories and improving cotton seeds. (Special Dispatch, 5th)

Japanese Ito in Europe 12

To Deal with Our Country's Blockade of the Puppet Post Office

(London) [Manchukuo] Because China does not receive mail sent from Manchuria, it has specially sent Ito, an advisor to the Ministry of Affairs, to Europe to find ways to speed up the delivery of mail from Siberia in Shanghai. Ito has met with the Post Office several times and discussed the issue of changing the distribution center from Dalian to Yuguan. Ito will go to Paris tomorrow to meet with French authorities and will return here later. (Reuters Dispatch, 4th)

Exhibition of Famous Chinese Paintings 13

Opening in Berlin on the 20th of This Month

(Berlin) The exhibition of famous Chinese paintings organized by Liu Haisu is scheduled to open on the 20th of this month at the Prussian Academy of Arts here. This is the first time that Chinese paintings have been officially exhibited in Germany. It is said that there are a total of 300 famous paintings. (National Power Dispatch, 8th)

Telegrams of Condolences from Chairman Lin and Others to the Wu Family 14

(Nanjing) Chairman Lin of the National Government sent a telegram of condolence to the family of Wu Chaoshu on the 5th, saying: To Wu Tiyun's residence, No. 3 Xinghan Road, Hong Kong, for the attention of Brother Shi. Upon receiving Mr. Sun Zhesheng's winter telegram, I was shocked and grieved to learn of the sudden passing of your esteemed father. Your esteemed father was always known for his loyalty and meritorious service to the Party and the nation. In these times of difficulty, the sudden withering of such a wise man is a cause of grief and regret shared by both China and foreign countries. I hope that Brother Shi will restrain your grief with propriety, diligently assist in important matters, and console the spirit of the deceased. I send this telegram of condolence. Lin Sen (5th) Seal, (5th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Zhang Ji sent a telegram to Hong Kong on the 5th to express condolences to the family of Wu Chaoshu, saying: I read in the newspaper with shock that Mr. Tiyun passed away from a brain ailment. We have only recently parted, and now the pillar has suddenly collapsed. Recalling our handshake in Hong Kong, I am overcome with sadness for a lost confidant. I hereby send this telegram of condolence and hope that you will restrain your grief. Zhang Ji (5th) (5th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Ju Zheng, President of the Judicial Yuan, sent a telegram of condolence to the family of Wu Chaoshu on the 4th, saying: I have just received the news of Mr. Tiyun's passing. Not only has our Party suffered a major loss, and comrades feel deep sorrow and regret, but all those with understanding cannot help but feel a shared grief. Public duty and private friendship, the loss of a man and the suffering of the nation, I send this telegram of condolence, expressing my sincere feelings. I humbly request that you restrain your grief and hope that you will consider this. (5th Central News Agency Telegram)

Yin Rugeng Goes to Tongzhou 15

Staying in Tongzhou for Three to Five Days Before Going to Tianjin

Requesting Instructions on the Dates of Inspection of Various Counties

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng, accompanied by Huo Shi and He Xiaoyi, went to Tongzhou by car this afternoon. According to reports, he will stay in Tongzhou for three to five days before going to Beiping and then to Tianjin to meet with Yu Xuezhong, requesting instructions on the dates of inspection of various counties. Regarding the issue of receiving Gubeikou, an initial agreement has been reached with the Japanese side, and the departure has been postponed. Of the passes along the Great Wall under the jurisdiction of the Jiji District, only Gubeikou and Malanyu are involved. After requesting instructions from Huang Zi on the procedures, further negotiations will be held with the Japanese side, and the reception can then be initiated without any major problems. This time, the Liu bandit troops caused great disturbance in Tongzhou, looting extremely cruelly. The local losses are currently being investigated to be presented for the allocation of funds for relief. (5th Special Telegram)

Annual Tax Revenue of Guangdong Province 16

Nearly Reaches 50 Million Yuan

(Guangzhou) According to official documents, since the implementation of the new tariff regulations, the annual tax revenue of Guangdong Province has nearly reached 50 million yuan. The total tax revenue last year was 48,992,218 yuan. Although tax revenue has increased and there are monthly subsidies from the central government, the financial situation of the provincial government remains extremely difficult. Therefore, new sources of tax revenue are being sought to compensate. It is noted that the provincial government's expenditure last year reached 49,092,179 yuan, with most of the provincial treasury being used for military and political purposes. Last year, taxes on kerosene, business, imported foreign rice, and other agricultural products were increased. (5th Reuters Telegram)

The Rome Conference Concludes; Britain and Italy Reach Complete Agreement

The Issue of Disarmament Should Be Resolved First

The Restructuring of the League of Nations Can Be Discussed Later

Mussolini Pays Attention to the Situation in the Pacific 22

●Rome The talks between British Foreign Secretary Simon and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini ended tonight. Both sides completely agreed that discussions on disarmament should be concluded as soon as possible, and that all proposals that cannot gain popular support or be implemented quickly should be discarded. A banquet was held at the British Embassy tonight, attended by members of the diplomatic corps and leaders of the Italian and British communities. After the banquet, a communique was issued stating that after two harmonious and lengthy talks, the two politicians believed that only points that international public opinion considered legitimate should be noted. Regarding the restructuring of the League of Nations, Mussolini reiterated his opinion, stating that the League of Nations must be restructured or allowed to perish. The Italian Prime Minister also said that if the major powers do not reach a proper agreement, the situation in the Pacific will evolve into an unavoidable war. It is heard that Simon is quite satisfied with the results of this trip. Simon is scheduled to return to London tomorrow. France and Germany are both closely watching the negotiations in Rome. According to news from Berlin citing an editorial in a certain newspaper, if France can fulfill its recently vaguely promised disarmament plan, everyone will be satisfied. It is noted that this newspaper usually represents the views of the German Foreign Ministry. Also, according to news from Paris, France is feeling somewhat unhappy because Britain and Italy now consider themselves to be mediators between France and Germany. (4th Reuters Telegram)

Britain and Italy Decide on the Most Urgent Issues in Europe 23

Simon Returns Home via Paris 24

●Rome It has been learned today that British Foreign Secretary Simon and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini have decided on the most urgent issues currently facing Europe, namely that a disarmament agreement should be established quickly and that the restructuring of the League of Nations should be relegated to secondary importance. The League of Nations must be restructured, but this should wait until the disarmament issue is resolved and the legitimate demands of France and Germany are satisfied. Furthermore, the restructuring of the League of Nations must aim to strengthen its structure. British Foreign Secretary Simon issued an article to reporters today, stating that he felt that politicians in all countries recognized that failure to reach a disarmament agreement would be detrimental to all countries. He had seen complete sincerity everywhere, and the talks in Rome and Paris were all of value. It is heard that the politicians did not discuss any actual plans for restructuring the League of Nations; only Mussolini briefly mentioned how the League of Nations should be reformed. British Foreign Secretary Simon departed from here today, taking the route through Paris to return to London. The proposals discussed in Rome will be submitted to the British government for consideration. (5th Reuters Telegram)

●Rome After meeting twice with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, British Foreign Secretary Simon told visiting reporters today that the issue of disarmament must be resolved first, and only then can other issues be considered. That is, restructuring the League of Nations is secondary to disarmament. Simon also stated that the Italian Prime Minister firmly believed that the current chaotic situation in Europe must be clarified as soon as possible to avoid serious threats to world peace. Simon further stated that while reforming the League of Nations is important, the politicians he met believed that disarmament should be resolved first. Regarding disarmament, he believed that Germany's spiritual equality and equal military armament should be recognized, and pointed out Article 26 of the Covenant, which stipulates amendment procedures, stating that the amendment can increase the strength of the League of Nations and the Covenant. He also stated that all the politicians with whom he had discussed these issues believed that if a war were to break out, no country in the world could escape the resulting suffering. (5th National Telegram)

Mussolini Supports Hitler's Demands 25

The League of Nations Issue Was Discussed at Length 26

●Rome It was reliably learned today that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, in his two talks with British Foreign Secretary Simon, supported several demands made by German Chancellor Hitler. Mussolini reiterated his long-held belief that Germany should be granted spiritual equality. The meaning of this move is to abolish the clause in the Treaty of Versailles that Germany was the aggressor. In addition, Mussolini also told Simon that the Germans should be granted the right to limited rearmament so that the prestige of the German people and the Hitler government could be maintained. In addition, the two also discussed at length Italy's proposal to restructure the League of Nations. Mussolini stated that the restructuring of the League of Nations should be implemented immediately after the disarmament issue is resolved. Today, the Italian Foreign Ministry issued a communique confirming that the two sides had discussed the issues of disarmament and restructuring the League of Nations. The communique stated that Mussolini's and Simon's two talks here studied the major issues related to the policy of restructuring the League of Nations. In addition, the limitation of armaments also received the closest attention. Both sides agreed that the disarmament negotiations should be concluded as soon as possible. Mussolini also put forward several outlines as a basis for restructuring the League of Nations, so that the organization could operate more flexibly and achieve its goals more easily. (4th National Telegram)

●Rome Last night, the British Embassy hosted a banquet for Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, and British Foreign Secretary Simon was present. He spoke especially with Italian Ambassador to Britain Grandi and the ambassadors of France, Germany, and the United States to Italy. Responsible parties believe that Mussolini's views on reforming the League of Nations can be implemented within the scope of the League's current Covenant. (5th Havas Telegram)

Soviet Russia Joins League of Nations; Italian Response 27

▲ Far Eastern Situation Promotes Change

▲ Japan's Isolation is the Merit of the League of Nations

●Moscow Since Molotov and Litvinov made their remarks a few days ago, general public opinion has recognized that these remarks are sufficient to show that Soviet Russia's attitude towards the League of Nations has recently changed greatly. Therefore, political and diplomatic circles are using the possibility of Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations as the sole basis for discussion. It is said that if Soviet Russia joins the League of Nations, it will be very suitable for Soviet Russia's long-proclaimed policy of peaceful cooperation. However, the biggest reason for the change in Soviet Russia's attitude is the situation in the Far East. Soviet Russia believes that Japan's isolation is the merit of the League of Nations, and Japan's isolated position has given a serious obstacle to the expansion of Japanese imperialism. Therefore, the League of Nations can also be called an important factor in maintaining peace in the Far East. For this reason, Soviet Russia has a strong intention to cooperate closely with the League of Nations, and the most natural way is to send a permanent observer to Geneva, and then request formal accession after a few days. (4th National Telegram)

League of Nations Executive Council Meeting on January 15

Promotes Germany's Return to the Disarmament Conference

(London) The diplomatic correspondent for the Daily Telegraph reports that British political circles believe that continued direct talks between France and Germany are not feasible at present. The differences of opinion between the two sides have been reduced by short-term contact, but it is difficult to hope for an early understanding without the cooperation of other major powers. The British government is now advocating convening a meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council on January 15, at which representatives from Britain, France, Italy, and the United States will study the situation of the Franco-German negotiations and the results of the Mussolini-Simon talks, study the disarmament issue, strive to accommodate Germany's views, and seek a general understanding so as to lead Germany back to the Disarmament Conference. Therefore, after the League of Nations Executive Council meets, the major powers will make new proposals to Germany, but this will depend on whether France agrees with Britain's approach. French Memorandum to Germany Still Emphasizes Universal Disarmament

Cannot Discuss Rearmament

(Paris) There has been much speculation about the content of the French memorandum sent to Germany on the issue of armaments. News from London claims to know the details of the memorandum. A certain local morning newspaper published it. According to this news, it seems that there is something new in the memorandum. However, according to what we have heard, and the news supplemented by reliable sources, it proves that the rumors from outside are all unfounded. In fact, the French government only stated in the memorandum that the Franco-German negotiations can only aim at universal disarmament, and cannot discuss German rearmament. The memorandum also explained the scope and conditions under which France itself is prepared to reduce its armaments. Roosevelt Asks Congress to Approve 29

Huge US Naval Shipbuilding Costs 30

Totaling 54 Million Yuan 31

Navy Personnel to Increase to 80,000

Army Adds 100 Fighter Planes

(Washington) The US Army Department announced today that it will immediately order 100 fighter planes for the Army, at a total cost of approximately 7.5 million yuan. This will be allocated from the 330 million yuan public works fund and will not be included in the next fiscal year's budget. Regarding the Navy, the US President listed 288,030,725 yuan in the next fiscal year's budget, of which 53,800,000 yuan will be used to continue the shipbuilding program. The number of naval personnel will increase from 79,700 to 82,500, and the Marine Corps will also expand from 15,000 to 16,000. (4th National Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt today asked Congress to approve 54 million yuan for naval construction, including the cost of building new warships, but not including 32 warships funded from the 238 million yuan public works fund. The 288 million yuan stipulated in the 1935 budget, together with the accumulated surplus from previous years, gives the Navy Department a total of 316 million yuan for shipbuilding and other expenses. In addition, 2.75 million yuan must be raised to increase naval personnel from 79,700 to 82,500, and the Marine Corps from 15,000 to 16,000. The Navy's air force funding is approximately 1 million yuan less than last year, but the 7 million yuan allocated by the public works fund can maintain the production of 1,000 aircraft. The Army's total funding is 294 million yuan, 15 million yuan more than this year, of which 10 million yuan is for increasing the Army's air force. (4th Reuters Telegram)

US Naval and Air Force Exercises in the Pacific 32

●San Diego Naval Port More than 100 US warships began exercises in the Pacific south of Catalina Island. Several squadrons of military aircraft and the giant airship Macon also participated in the exercises. (4th Havas Telegram)

The Scale of the Budget is Frightening

(Washington) Judging from the US budget, President Roosevelt wants to spend a total of 840 million yuan on various projects from today until the end of the fiscal year at the end of June. The scale of this number is unprecedented in peacetime. The government estimates that its revenue in the next 18 months is based on a 34 percent increase in industrial production during this period. The budget director and comptroller have the power to supervise temporary spending. House Speaker Rainey, referring to this budget, said that the deficit in the budget is truly alarming. House Republican Leader Snell said that he was shocked to hear of the amount of money the authorities intended to use. However, Senator Reed said that the people would definitely be able to bear the burden of 310 million yuan without worry.

Treasury Deficit of 600 Million Yuan

(Washington) The US Treasury Department today issued its annual report, stating that by the end of the fiscal year on June 30, the Treasury will have a deficit of 6,621,239,711 yuan, which, except during wartime, is the largest deficit in American history. The total national debt will reach 28,679,969,728 yuan, also an unprecedented debt. This is because it is expected that relief spending will increase month by month in the next six months, increasing the monthly deficit by 100 million yuan. The total expenditure of the national treasury for the whole year will reach 9,891,178,467 yuan. Only the wartime expenditures of 1918 and 1919 exceeded this number. The total revenue for the whole year will be 3,259,938,756 yuan. It is estimated that regular government expenses account for only 3,533,691,767 yuan of the total expenditure, and the rest is relief and reconstruction expenses. The Financial Reconstruction Corporation alone spent 3,969,740,000 yuan, followed by the principal and interest on the national debt, which also reached 742 million yuan. As for the Army, it only spent 61,880,800 yuan, and the Navy only spent 56,063,200 yuan. Compared with the previous two items, it is like a small witch compared to a big witch. As for the Treasury's income, various domestic stamp taxes are the most, accounting for 41 percent of the total income. On the other hand, income tax accounts for only 36 percent, the lowest tax revenue in nine years. The estimated regular expenditures for the next fiscal year ending June 30, 1935, are only 4,486,562,500 yuan, including Army expenses of 62,007,700 yuan and Navy expenses of 288,030,725 yuan. The estimated revenue for that year is 3,974,665,479 yuan. (4th National Telegram)

New Delhi Conference: India-Japan Agreement Established 36

To Begin Drafting a New Trade Agreement

To Be Formally Signed in Ten Days

Japanese Businesses to Cancel Boycott of Indian Cotton

Conditional on Reducing Tariffs

◎New Delhi: The final meeting of the India-Japan conference was held at noon on the 5th, attended by all representatives from both sides. The establishment of the India-Japan Agreement has been confirmed. (5th Jiji News Agency)

(Tokyo) The India-Japan conference formally finalized all the items discussed on the 5th. At the same time, it was decided to abolish the boycott of Indian cotton and implement a reduction in cotton cloth tariffs. Therefore, the India-Japan Agreement can be said to have officially come to an end in fact. However, the drafting committee composed of representatives from both countries will begin work on the treaty on the 6th to complete it as soon as possible. However, the return of Governor Bowra is expected around the 9th. The draft must be initialed by both parties, and then the document will be mailed to Mr. Matsudaira, the Japanese ambassador in London, and Foreign Minister Simon for their signatures. The British side has already stated that it will not interfere in any decisions made by India and Japan. Therefore, this India-Japan trade treaty should be able to be announced in late January or early February. The above signature is only a formality, and the effect of the treaty will in fact occur simultaneously with the temporary initialing. It is reported that the Japanese government and private representatives will withdraw immediately after the temporary initialing. (5th Jiji News Agency)

●New Delhi: Today's India-Japan plenary meeting was held here at noon (3:30 PM Japan time). All the negotiated items were endorsed and passed. Because the negotiated items have been contacted in advance, they must be implemented as soon as possible. Therefore, the following three items will be provisionally initialed: (1) The Japanese side cancels the boycott of Indian cotton, (2) The Indian government reduces cotton cloth tariffs to 50%, or 5 annas and a quarter per pound, (3) Simultaneously implement the distribution of cotton cloth imports. It was decided to implement it from the 8th and issue a declaration in the form of minutes of the meeting, signed by representatives Sawada and Bowra. The meeting ended at 0:40 PM. The full text of the minutes will be released simultaneously in Tokyo and New Delhi on the afternoon of the 6th. (5th Dentsu News Agency)

●New Delhi: A special correspondent reported that the India-Japan plenary meeting, which opened at noon on the 5th, should formally confirm the agreed matters. The content is roughly as follows: It covers all the issues that have been agreed upon, regarding the most-favored-nation treatment clause, (1) the clause that the two countries should negotiate when making general tariff revisions, (1) the exchange rate clause, (1) the clause on increasing cotton cloth tax rates, (1) the clause on cotton cloth import ratios, (1) the clause on the separation of Burma, (1) the clause on the effective period of import ratios. In this agreement clause, regarding the tariff of the Darwan (达运?) export principle, except for Goa, there are currently about 4.5 million yards of cotton cloth stored in bonded warehouses, so the benefits received by the Japanese side are not small. (4th Dentsu News Agency)

Matsudaira's Talk

(London) Today, Matsudaira, the Japanese ambassador to the UK, told a Reuters reporter about the India-Japan cotton industry agreement, saying that the atmosphere for the start of British-Japanese negotiations should be more satisfactory than before. The British often attribute the sluggish trade to Japanese competition. Now that the trade situation is gradually improving in the new year, the British should have a more reasonable attitude. Matsudaira mentioned the low price level, saying that a bicycle worth one pound and a hat worth fifteen pence will definitely not be durable. Japanese people like British goods because they are durable. He also said that Japanese businessmen are very willing to resolve peacefully and avoid tariff wars, so the European war will destroy the old friendship between Britain and Japan. After the establishment of the India-Japan agreement, some people are worried that halving the tariffs will give Japanese goods a great price advantage, but Lancashire businessmen welcome this agreement for the following reasons: (1) British-Japanese conferences can start immediately, (2) Japanese goods imported into India are ultimately limited, (3) The Indian government is now free to conclude British-Indian agreements on cotton and rayon. Lancashire is therefore now preparing various plans. (4th Reuters)

British Newspaper Commentary

(London) The Financial News today commented on the India-Japan cotton industry agreement, saying that this kind of agreement is indeed needed, but at most it will only prevent the cotton industry problem from expanding. The original difficulties of Lancashire still exist. Its very important major market in the East, which it has always supplied, is now completely self-sufficient or an active exporter. No matter what the content of the agreement, the agreement has been established after all. This is the key point, otherwise the competition will be more intense and the animosity will be deeper. (5th Reuters)

Tragic Situation After the Sui County Disaster

(Nanjing) Liu Xiang telegraphed Chairman Chiang and President Wang, according to Fan Shaozeng's telegram, Sui County was recovered. The bandit's brutal behavior was surveyed by dispatched personnel, according to the report: (1) After the bandits entered the city, they looted civilian goods. An economic store was set up on each street, forcing people to buy. Those who did not accept were killed. (2) Those who have not retreated and are able to make a living are often identified as spies and ordered to redeem their sins with money. After paying the money, they are still killed at night. (3) Young men and women in the city and suburbs were all forced to serve as guerrilla pioneers and comfort teams. When they collapsed, they forced the people to go with them. Only the old, weak, and disabled were left. (4) All official documents, files, registers, books, boxes, and public property in official agencies, organs, and schools in the city were burned and nothing remained. (5) Clothes in houses on all streets were swept away, the four walls were desolate, no one was in sight, horse manure was everywhere, and weeds were a foot high, which was unbearable to see. (6) Deep pits were dug in Xunmen (勋门?) training grounds, river sand dams, various official offices, public offices, and supervisory offices, burying dozens or hundreds of male and female corpses. Today, another deep pit was found in the training ground, containing more than 20 female corpses wearing girls' school uniforms. No less than a thousand old and weak people with hoes were identifying the bodies, crying to the sky, and the stench was spreading everywhere. The fire was set along the street, and the essence was almost burned. With no clothes, no food, and no lodging, people are in great pain. The tragic situation is ten times worse than that of Jiangxi and western Hubei. (5th Central News Agency)
