Public Telegram 60

●Telegram from Zhengzhou: To the Shen Bao Newspaper,

Upon reading your newspaper's January 2nd combined issue, it was stated that on the 28th, coal cars on this line overturned in Sishui, severely injuring 17 passengers and railway workers. This is inconsistent with the facts. It has been verified that there were no passengers on the car, and no employees were injured. It was completely repaired on the same day and resumed normal operation. The reason for the derailment was that all the cars were foreign cars, and the size and condition were different. When encountering the initial snow, the tracks were slippery. When passing through the Xiapo (下破?) Great Bay, one car was squeezed off the track, and the remaining cars were pulled off the track, but they did not overturn, so the repairs were very fast. Due to inaccurate information, we hereby request a correction. Please do so accordingly. Sincerely, Longhai Railway Administration.

Japanese Troops Invading Chahar Build Large-Scale Airfield 61

And Build a Motor Road from Hada Camp to Yanqing

Four Japanese Aircraft Suddenly Bomb Chicheng

Beiping correspondence: The Japanese troops invading eastern Chahar have decided not to withdraw due to concerns about Russia. Recently, in addition to establishing a bandit suppression headquarters in Heihe, they have also built a large-scale airfield in Hada Camp in the second and fourth districts of Guyuan. It has now been completed and 24 aircraft are stationed there. A motor road 18 feet wide is also being built, running directly from Hada Camp to Yanqing. It has already started. Yanqing is the western border line of the war zone, only 25 li away from Kangzhuang. This kind of action by the Japanese army contains great conspiracies. The Chahar provincial authorities have already telegraphed the Beiping authorities to make representations to the Japanese side. In addition, after Liu Guitang's troops left Chicheng, the Japanese army suddenly dispatched four aircraft on the 2nd and 3rd to inspect the defense area of the Chahar army Zhang Yuanrong's troops in the Chicheng Yongning area and dropped dozens of bombs back and forth. The Chahar provincial authorities also telegraphed Beiping for instructions. The Beiping Military Branch will send Zhu Shiqin to visit the Japanese embassy military attache Hobon to inquire. The military attache replied that they were bombing the bandit troops of Liu Guitang's unit. Zhu immediately told him that Liu's troops had fled south. Hobon agreed to convey this to the Japanese Kwantung Army and stop bombing. The actions of the Japanese army in eastern Chahar are becoming increasingly strange, and their intentions are difficult to fathom. (January 4th)

Liu Guitang's Troops Disturb Northern Beiping 62

Intending to Cross Southern Beiping and Flee to Shandong and Henan

Troops Stationed in Various Places Strictly Block and Attack

Beiping correspondence: After Liu Guitang's troops defected and left Chicheng, they actually raised the banner of the Second Army of the East Asia Collaboration Army. They fled through Yongning and Yanqing towards the war zone. In advance, they sent representatives to contact the Japanese Kwantung Army, claiming that they were being oppressed by the Chahar army and could not gain a foothold in Chahar, requesting to enter the war zone and seek temporary protection. The Japanese side rejected this, replying that if they invaded the war zone, they would be dealt with. Since Liu was rejected, after fleeing to Erdaoguan, he did not dare to directly enter the war zone. Instead, he followed in the footsteps of Fang Ji and moved south along the edge of the war zone. At 4:00 PM on December 31st, they fled near the Ming Tombs Dahongmen between Changping and Nankou. After the authorities received news that Liu's troops were trying to enter the war zone, in addition to ordering the Chahar army to track and pursue, they also ordered the troops stationed in the Changping Nankou area to strictly block and, at the same time, ordered the security team in the war zone to guard the border of the war zone. The Changping Ming Tombs area is defended by Zhu Hongxun's 130th Division of Wan Fulin's army. When Liu's troops fled near the Ming Tombs, they clashed with a certain regiment of Zhu's division in the Dahongmen area. At dawn on New Year's Day, Liu's troops launched a surprise attack on Zhu's division, copying from Dahongmen to the Great and Small Tangshan, attempting to bypass Changping. The situation was extremely fierce. After fierce fighting for several hours, both sides suffered heavy casualties. Liu's troops fled into the Tangshan market town and looted wildly. At about 2:00 PM, Zhu's division attacked from the east of Changping towards the east, and Guan Linzheng's division of the Central Army blocked from Mafang towards the north. After fierce fighting until about 5:00 PM, Liu's troops could not hold out and fled in droves from the eastern mountains and rivers. That night, they passed north of Mafang and fled into Shunyi County. At about 6:00 AM on the 2nd, a portion fled to Shilibu, 12 li south of Shunyi County, and came into contact with a certain regiment of Liu Duoquan's 105th Division. A portion suddenly arrived in the Niulanshan Gaoliying area, looting along the way. The residents suffered terrible devastation. The authorities ordered the troops stationed in northern Beiping to jointly encircle and suppress them. Liu Duoquan's troops and Li Xingcun's division of Shang Zhen's troops all went out to encircle from three sides. Liu's troops were mostly cavalry, running east and west, and their whereabouts were erratic. On the morning of that day, the remnants of Liu's troops in the Great and Small Tangshan area were completely cleared. There was still a portion in the Niulanshan Gaoliying area, which was being surrounded and dealt with. However, at about 3:00 PM that afternoon, dozens of Liu's cavalry suddenly arrived in Dongba, near Tongzhou, northern Beiping, wantonly burning and looting, and clashed with the local security team. At about 5:00 PM, government troops arrived from Yujiawei and scattered them. At about 8:00 PM that night, Liu's troops in that area began to flee towards Gaoqiao. On that day, they fled to Gaoqiao Shuangqiao at night. The Beiping military and police, because the bandits were only a dozen li from the city, sent troops to block them in the eastern suburbs and stepped up the city's defenses. On the 3rd, Liu's troops fled south through Dawangzhuang towards Hadian. Dozens more fled to the southern suburbs at night. The 105th Division stationed there blocked them. Gunfire broke out for a long time, and it could be heard very clearly in the city. After an hour, Liu's troops fled west along the Yongding River. On the 4th, the national army had gone to both banks of the Yongding River to pursue. The main force of Liu's troops fleeing east from northern Beiping was about 3,000 people. Also, on the morning of the 3rd, when Liu's troops invaded Wuqing County, they came into contact with the troops stationed there. Liu's troops were determined to flee and did not dare to linger. At about 11:00 AM, they crossed the railway and fled to Anci. They were blocked again by the troops stationed there. On the morning of the 4th, they had fled to Yin'an, attempting to escape to Puyang, Caozhou, and other places through the counties in southern Hebei. The Hebei Provincial Government has ordered the troops stationed in the counties of southern Hebei to work with the local militia security teams to strictly block them and send Bai Fengxiang's cavalry to pursue them, striving to encircle and resolve them in the shortest possible time.

On the 4th, Wang Yizhe, commander of the 67th Army, and the staff office of the army both sent telegrams to Beiping, reporting on the situation of blocking and suppressing Liu's troops. The telegrams are as follows: (1) Wang's telegram stated that Liu Guitang's bandit troops of more than 3,000 people fled to Anci at 3:00 AM on the 3rd, suddenly crossed the Beining Railway south between Aigezhuang and Wanzhuang in Langfang, robbing and killing along the way. Yue Rusheng, commander of the 650th Regiment of the 117th Division, led his troops to pursue, and Liu's bandits fled and scattered south. When they arrived at Dawulong Village, they were again severely attacked by Chen Enling, commander of the 2nd Battalion of the regiment, capturing more than 40 bandits, seizing 40 to 50 horses and mules, and more than 30 guns, and killing more than 80 bandits. The remnants of the bandits, about 50 or 60, changed into plain clothes at Yongledian, south of Tongxian, at 2:00 PM on the 3rd, and fled east across the Bai River. Zhu Zirong, commander of the 620th Regiment of the 107th Division, has dispatched more than 100 cavalry to pursue them. Another remnant force of about 300 to 400 people entrenched in the four villages of Maojiaying and Zhangjiawu in Anci County at 6:00 PM on the 3rd. Su Chengmou, commander of the 2nd Battalion of the 649th Regiment of the 117th Division, is leading his troops to pursue. The bandits have fled towards Gu'an. (2) The staff office telegraphed that after more than 2,000 Liu's bandits were defeated in Dawulong Village on the 3rd, they fled towards the Yongding River bank. Wang Zhihan, commander of the 694th Regiment of the 117th Division, led his troops to pursue and advanced towards Gu'an. Liu Hanyu, commander of the 628th Regiment of the 107th Division, led his troops to pursue from Jiuzhou Town towards the north bank of the Yongding River. The 629th Regiment of the 110th Division was stationed in Hanzhuang to block them. The 3rd Company of the Armored Train patrolled between Langfang and Anding. Liu's bandits attempted to flee to Henan and join the Communist bandits.

Xia Ziming's brigade of Liu's troops broke away from Liu at the beginning of Liu's defection and remained stationed in the original defense of Longmensuo, declaring their obedience to the orders of the Chahar Provincial Government. Chairman Song Zheyuan of Chahar, considering that Xia was deeply aware of righteousness, has submitted a request to the Beiping Military Commission to reorganize Xia's troops into a brigade, consisting of one cavalry regiment and two infantry regiments. Xia's troops will be paid with the original salary of Liu's troops. (4th)

Mr. Sun Yat-sen's Talk While Passing Through Manila (Philippines Correspondence) 63

Amidst this period of both external and internal troubles, the news suddenly came that Mr. Sun Yat-sen, the President of the Legislative Yuan, would be taking a short trip to Manila. On the morning of December 23rd, he arrived in Manila aboard the President Hoover. Accompanying him were his wife and two sons, as well as former Air Force Commander Zhang Huichang, former Minister of Finance Huang Hanliang, Legislative Yuan member Wu Jingxiong, and Secretary Yu Ming, along with several others. After disembarking, Mr. Sun immediately went to the Consulate General to meet with Chinese and foreign reporters. He made the following statement to the Western press reporters: "[After the Philippines becomes independent, it should pay close attention to the ambitions of the Japanese Empire. Japan will definitely act as it did in Manchuria, first invading the Philippines with economic power, and then overcoming it politically. Japan is constantly watching the Philippines, and the Philippines is very suitable for Japanese development]," he said.

Regarding the Fujian Incident, Mr. Sun said that Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, and even the 19th Route Army were merely occupying Fujian to carry out their political movements, which had nothing to do with the people of Fujian. This was because the 19th Route Army was a Guangdong army, not a local Fujian army. The biggest problem with the Chinese people is their inability to cooperate. The leaders are divided due to regional, historical, and personal feelings, leading to a state of political turmoil. Furthermore, soldiers like to interfere in politics, preventing politics from getting on the right track. It's like a car where the soldiers are the drivers and the people are the passengers. Now, the passengers have no way to order the driver to drive to the destination.

Page 10

If the driver drives the car erratically, wouldn't China be in trouble? Regarding the issue of suppressing the communists, Mr. Sun said that the previous methods of suppressing the communists were inappropriate, which is why they failed. Progress has now been made, and the root of the matter is entirely an economic problem. Regarding the issue of resisting Japan, he said that the government is not unwilling to resist Japan, but because China is so internally divided, and everyone is not cooperating, and politics is such a mess, and the country's power is so weak, how can we resist?

That evening, the General Branch of the Kuomintang and the Manila Chinese Chamber of Commerce held a banquet for Mr. Sun and his party at the Great Eastern Hotel, presided over by Consul General Kuang. Chen Sanduo, Chairman of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce, described in detail the recent bombings of Zhangzhou and Quanzhou by airplanes, and presented Mr. Sun with a written petition. Mr. Sun immediately read it carefully, looking extremely concerned. The chairman then invited Mr. Sun to give a speech. Mr. Sun said that this was his third time coming to the Philippines and that this time it was purely for travel and did not carry any mission. He felt ashamed to receive such a warm welcome from the overseas Chinese tonight, but he was fortunate to have the opportunity to meet and talk with everyone. The overseas Chinese here are enthusiastic and patriotic, and they are particularly concerned about the Fujian Incident and must be eager to understand it. Therefore, he would like to report to the overseas Chinese what he knows about the recent situation in China. Overseas Chinese have no more than two types of mindsets: one is dissatisfied with the current situation, and the other hopes that in the future, all parties can unite to form a strong and powerful government to turn the tide and improve the country's situation. Both of these mindsets are what patriots should have. Those in authority are often confused, while observers are clear. Moreover, our government is a government of the people, so of course everyone can speak out, so that the government knows where its mistakes are and can follow the path of improvement. Since the success of the Northern Expedition, there has been no achievement in politics in the past twenty-two years, which is undeniable. However, is this kind of mistake due to the fact that the Three Principles of the People are insufficient to save China and are not suitable for China's situation? In my honest opinion, it is not that the Three Principles of the People are insufficient to save China, but that the central government is unable to implement them. Since the success of the Northern Expedition, the party has been divided, and there have been years of civil war. In the past, the campaigns against Yan Xishan and Feng Yuxiang, and even the recent Fujian Incident, had to resort to military force. Moreover, this kind of civil war cannot be blamed solely on the old warlords, nor can it be blamed solely on the central government. The biggest problem is that internal divisions arise and cannot be united. If there is no unity, the power of the central government is weak and it cannot implement policies to seek progress. Now, the central government has sent Zhang Ji, Ma Chaojun, Wang Luyi, and Chen Zhaoying, four people, to contact Hu Hanmin and the southwestern provinces, precisely to seek unity. Hu has been living in Hong Kong for the past two years, and has repeatedly made detailed criticisms and severe accusations of the national government's military and political arrangements. In fact, mere accusations are useless. If everyone can plan for unity, then Nanjing will humbly listen to advice and accept the contributions of the southwest. In short, the way to save the country is for all parties to cooperate sincerely. Hu issued a declaration the other day, putting forward eight propositions, and when I was in Hong Kong, newspaper reporters sought my opinion. Although I have not read the full text, its eight propositions are all suitable for saving the country, and I fully agree with them. Mr. Sun also said that Hu Hanmin advocates resisting Japan, and the words "resisting Japan" should be agreed upon by the entire nation. However, in order to implement it, we must first think about how to do it. If we want to gather the national army and go to the Northeast, and make a desperate gamble, it would be too risky. Therefore, we must first strengthen the country's power, and then be prepared for war. Appropriately, the Chamber of Commerce requested to relay a telegram to prevent the bombing of southern Fujian. When this matter first happened, I was still in Nanjing and received telegrams from various places, requesting a halt. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek had also instructed the air force to pay attention and not to indiscriminately bomb civilians. As for the second time, I don't know. The Chamber of Commerce represents the opinions of all overseas Chinese, and I will immediately relay this intention to the central military authorities.

### The Sichuan Army Recaptures Yilong and Qianjiang 64

丨丨Remnant Bandits on the Border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Flee to Southern Henan 丨丨

Hankou Correspondence: Since the Sichuan bandit suppression army recovered Sui and Xuan, the military center of gravity has shifted to Yilong. Tian Songyao, the commander of the Second Route Army, also generously took on the responsibility of recovering Yilong after Chiang Kai-shek repeatedly urged him to fight. According to reports, the Li Weiruyi unit of the right wing army of this route recovered Yicheng on the 1st of this month. The remaining forces of Xu Xiangqian retreated to Tongjiang and Bazhong. He Long's bandit forces entered Sichuan and colluded with the Lianyinghui bandits to capture the county seat of Qianjiang in eastern Sichuan, and repeatedly committed westward offenses, attempting to join forces with the Xu bandits. The militia fought hard to resist, but failed. Recently, due to the defeat and retreat of the Xu bandits, their momentum has become even more isolated. Liu Xiang, the commander-in-chief of the Sichuan bandit suppression, specially transferred the Peng brigade of the First Division and the Da brigade of the First Division to take the opportunity to attack and suppress them, and also recovered Qiancheng on the 1st. According to a telegram from Liu Xiang, the bandits are now fleeing to Daluba and Longping, and he is ordering various units to pursue and suppress them. The crisis in Sichuan has been slightly eased as a result.

The remnant bandits on the border of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui are now few and far between. Liu Zhenhua, the commander-in-chief, telegraphed on the 4th, saying that they are all fleeing into Gushi, southern Henan. The 65th Division of Liu Maoen and the 45th Division of Dai Minquan have been ordered to encircle and suppress them, and have repeatedly won victories. Liu's unit killed the false brigade commander Li Furen and the false regimental commander Lang Zefu. Dai's unit recovered Wulongji, Huolonggang, Caomiaoji, Quhe, Quanhepu, and Zhangguangmiao, and pursued the bandits to Jianshan. A unit of the false 82nd Division, entrenched in Zhanglaobu, Dafoshan, and Yanling, was also defeated by the Tan brigade of this division. The following is Dai Minquan's victory telegram: "[According to a telegram from Brigade Commander Tan, the bandits who disturbed Zhanglaobu plundered grain yesterday morning and fled successively to Yingheji and Yangjiaji in the south. At the same time, the bandits entrenched in Dacha Shop collected kerosene and firewood, claiming to burn down the bridges on the highway, and transported grain and grass to Peijiachong in the south. The bandits at Qingfengling were withdrawn to Dafoshan and Yanling to guard against our army's pursuit. According to reports, I ordered Yang's regiment at Wumiao Ji, Chen's camp at Suxianshi, and Zhu's camp at Zaoxiehe to intercept them in different directions, and engaged in mixed battles with the bandits at Wangjialou, Suokou, Yanling, and Peijiachong. Our Zhu's camp launched a fierce attack on the bandits at Yanling, engaging in hand-to-hand combat and charging, and occupied Yanling. The bandits fled to Yiyuan Temple, and the remaining bandits wavered and fled in different directions to Changjiang River and Shimenkou. Our Yang's regiment and Zhu's camp tracked them to Yangjiaji Yiyuan Temple. Due to the late hour and rain, each returned to its original defense. An inspection of the abandoned bandit corpses revealed one false 82nd Division regimental commander, Li Tengxiao, and 91 guns and dozens of bags of grain were seized. It is believed that the bandits have been exhausted after this attack. Our special suppression units should take advantage of their lack of breath to quickly suppress them. It is expected that it will not be difficult to annihilate them. I respectfully report this, Dai Minquan, [seal]," (January 4th)

### Stability in the Recovered Bandit Areas of Hubei Province 65

Regulations for Rent and Debt Relief Announced Widely

Issuance of Financial Bonds to Implement Economic Construction

Hankou Correspondence: Zhang Qun, Chairman of the Hubei Provincial Government, believes that the people in the recovered bandit areas have suffered greatly from the bandits for a long time, and are in extreme pain. They have no time to save the dead, and it is inevitable that they will be unable to pay rent and repay debts. In order to seek stability, he specially followed the principles instructed by Chiang Kai-shek and stipulated two measures as follows: (1) In all newly recovered bandit areas of various counties, the rice and grain of the 22nd year will all be harvested by the tenant farmers who planted them. (2) Regardless of new or old debts, they will all be extended to after the autumn harvest of the 23rd year for settlement. An order was issued on the 4th, and landlords and creditors were notified of the general situation, urging them not to violate the order and demand repayment, causing disturbances. In addition, in order to seek economic construction, Zhang plans to implement a plan starting this year. The largest amount of money is needed for sorting out the debt of armor, recovering the official property of Shengcheng Lane. The provincial treasury does not have this financial capacity, so it was decided to issue financial bonds of 4 million yuan, to be used for distribution. The rental income of public property in the province and the dividend of the provincial bank will be used as the principal and interest repayment fund. If there is a shortfall, it will be allocated from the business tax and submitted to the provincial bank for storage on a monthly basis. The face value is divided into 10,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan, with an annual interest rate of 6%, and the principal and interest will be repaid every six months, and all will be repaid in twelve years. This bond can be issued after it is passed by the Legislative Yuan and approved by the General Headquarters. (4th)

### Decline of Guangdong's Commerce in the Past Year 66

Foreign Trade Plummeted

Inland Industry and Commerce Suffered Losses and Decline

Guangzhou Correspondence: The commerce of Guangdong Province throughout the 22nd year showed a state of decline, which was unprecedented in decades. The general situation of various industries in the past year is briefly described as follows: (1) Foreign Trade: Shunde and Nanhai counties in Guangdong Province have always been known for their large-scale exports of raw silk. Last year, the export volume decreased sharply. In previous years, the monthly export volume was always above 7,000 packages, but last year, the monthly export volume was only more than 1,000 packages. At the same time, silk prices plummeted. Normally, the price of silk per dan (100 catties) is about 1,000 yuan, but last year, the price fell to 500 yuan, or even 300 yuan. Hundreds of thousands of male and female silk reeling workers in Shunde lost their jobs. The export volume of other products such as tea, tobacco, silk scarves, Gu embroidery, ivory utensils, and jade objects also plummeted. As for imported goods, Guangdong Province used to be a major sales market for foreign goods. Recently, due to the increase in tariffs, the prices of foreign cloth and wool are still high, and people's purchasing power has decreased. Therefore, more than a dozen large cloth shops went bankrupt last year. (2) Inland Commerce: The prosperity of Guangzhou City has always been measured by the development of the silver industry. However, last year, the silver industry in Guangzhou almost completely collapsed. The reasons are: first, the silk industry declined, and there were no loan opportunities; second, the business of various Jiang groceries shops (commonly known as the Sanjiang Gang) declined, and there was very little mortgage lending to silver shops; third, it was affected by the trend of low and falling paper money; fourth, the rich have weak faith in silver shops and dare not deposit money, only withdraw money, especially when the paper money trend occurred. Last year, the silver industry was greatly affected by the above factors, so more than 70 large and small silver shops went bankrupt, owing a total of more than 6 million yuan to outsiders. Fortunately, in November, the government announced restrictions on depositors' withdrawals, and those who had not received benefits were able to barely survive, but they were also heavily indebted. As for the rice industry, last year, due to the continuous decline in the price of foreign rice, and the once imposed tax on foreign rice, the entire industry suffered losses. The losses of rice shops were 200,000 to 300,000 yuan for the large ones, and more than 100,000 yuan for the upper ones. The situation of decline was unprecedented in the past 30 years. As for the Sanjiang Gang, such as the miscellaneous grain shops, rice and sugar shops, sugar and flour shops, and oil and bean shops, they were affected by the decline of various industries, and also faced the Taikoo Wheel strike. The losses of various industries were no less than 1 million yuan, and the number of shops that suffered losses reached nine out of ten. In recent years, real estate construction in Guangzhou has been prosperous for a while, and many speculators have become rich. Unexpectedly, since the second half of last year, changes have occurred in the financial world, and funds have been short. Almost no one is interested in buildings. At the same time, building materials such as bricks, tiles, wood, stone, and cement have all fallen in price, and property prices have also fallen by 40% compared to normal times. The real estate companies' existing properties cannot be sold, and the losses can be imagined. Since society is so depressed, emerging industries have also been greatly affected. The native cloth woven in the interior was sold to the Nanyang area, but last year, the Nanyang business had not yet recovered, and the purchasing power of the people in the interior was weak. Therefore, dozens of native cloth weaving factories went bankrupt, and more than 5,000 male and female workers lost their jobs. In addition, more than half of the upper-made match factories also went bankrupt, and only 18 are left, with a 50% reduction in output. The native-made kerosene factories are squeezed out by foreign merchants, and only dozens are left, compared to more than 150 at the peak, only one-third are left and weak. In recent years, although the government and people's organizations have actively promoted the use of domestic goods, the silk industry could have taken the opportunity to flourish, but the people's livelihood is difficult and they cannot afford to buy them. Therefore, more than a dozen silk shops in Guangzhou also went bankrupt last year, and only one in a hundred can make a profit. (January 2nd)

### Jiaoji Railway's Profit Last Year Was 4 Million Yuan 67

Jinan Correspondence: Ge Guangting, chairman of the Jiaoji Railway Committee, is currently meeting with Han Fuju, chairman of the provincial government, for business. He took the Jiaoji Railway's 5th train west this morning (3rd) and arrived in Jinan at 6 pm. At the same time, Shi Han, director of the railway police department, also came to Jinan. Chairman Han Fuju and Mayor Wen Chenglie both welcomed him at the station. After getting off the train, Ge and Han went to Jinan Hotel to rest. According to Ge, the operating conditions of the Jiaoji Railway last year were not bad. According to the year-end settlement results last year, there was a surplus of more than 5 million this year. After repaying the Japanese debt of 1.2 million, there was still a surplus of more than 4 million. This number is not easy to obtain, and it may be difficult to repeat this in the future. This is because the sales of various local products in Qingdao are sluggish, freight volume has decreased, and income has been greatly affected. At present, peanuts are piled up everywhere, but they cannot be sold. The previous selling price was 13 or 14 yuan per 100 catties, but now it has fallen to about 4 yuan. In addition, tobacco leaves have also fallen in price. In total, tobacco farmers suffered losses of more than 10 million last year, etc. (3rd)

### Shandong Coal Industry Organizes Production and Sales Company 68

Intended to Rescue the Coal Industry

Government Sends Personnel for Guidance

Boshan Correspondence: Shandong is extremely rich in coal reserves. For more than ten years, it has occupied the center of gravity of China's coal production, especially Boshan. There are as many as twenty coal mining companies. In addition to supplying fuel to the province, it is also transported to Shanghai, Fujian, Guangdong, and the Yangtze River Basin, occupying the most important position in the province's export goods. After the September 18th Incident, the Japanese seized the coal mines in the Northeast, worked hard to exploit them, and dumped them everywhere. The domestic coal industry was greatly affected. Because foreign coal is sold at low prices, the cost of producing coal in this province is very high, and it cannot compete with it. The sales channels have been almost completely taken away. Even those who reluctantly sell it all bear the pain and lose money. The coal mining industry is on the verge of bankruptcy, and the local economy is declining as a result. Qingdao's exports are stagnant, and the market is also deserted due to the coldness of the wharf. Shen Honglie, the mayor of Qingdao, has noticed this and has specially consulted with the Shandong Provincial Government to discuss rescue methods. Zhang Honglie, director of the Department of Construction, has therefore gone to Qingdao to discuss methods with Mayor Shen and coal miners. The general opinion is to form a cooperative organization by coal miners to classify coal quality, grade it, and set prices in order to gain credibility and facilitate sales. This company is entirely organized by the business side. The government only sends personnel to provide guidance and supervision, and sets a deadline of one month to complete the organization. Major coal mining companies will meet in Boshan in the coming days to discuss organizational methods, and the provincial government and the municipal government will each send two people to Boshan to participate in the meeting in order to explain the meaning of organizing cooperation. It is purely to rescue the coal industry and the local economy, so as not to let the business side misunderstand that the government has other intentions. The provincial government has appointed Yu Wuheng, a technician from the Department of Construction, and Huang Yongtai, director of the Second Mining Bureau. The Qingdao Municipal Government has appointed Dong Zhidao, chief of the second section of the Social Affairs Bureau, and Ke Yuan Chuan Gentian. The four people arrived in Boshan yesterday (29th) and contacted the business side. The business side has decided to appoint Ding Jingchen, manager of Yuesheng Coal Mining Company, Liang Xisan, manager of Yonghe Coal Mining Company, and Yu Zijing, manager of Dongfang Coal Company as representatives to discuss organizational methods. Except for Liang Xisan of Yonghe Company, who is currently in Qingdao and has not yet arrived in Boshan, the others are all in Boshan. As soon as Liang Xisan arrives in Boshan, a formal meeting will be held to discuss it.

According to sources from the mining industry, Mayor Shen had already discussed the matter of organizing a cooperative company in the spring of the 22nd year, and entrusted Ding Jingchen, manager of Yuesheng Company, to draft an outline of the organization and solicit opinions from various colleagues. At that time, all companies expressed sympathy for this kind of organization, but many believed that the event was too large and the organization was not easy, so it was put on hold. Now that the government has taken the lead, most businessmen and people feel grateful. However, there are a few companies that do not want this organization under the conditions of personal interests due to their own special circumstances, but the number of this kind of company is very small and there is not much resistance. The government is quite determined. If the merchants themselves cannot organize it, they will organize it with the power of the government, etc.

In addition, when Ding Jingchen first proposed cooperation, he compiled the origin and general outline of the convention and printed and distributed it to colleagues. The origin states four benefits: (1) A unified agency can save expenses; (2) Unified goods can improve foreign credibility; (3) Due to the adjustment of goods, joint research and improvement can be carried out; (4) Small capital miners can obtain an equal position. The main points of its covenants are as follows: (1) Miners who join the cooperation should deliver all the coal produced to the cooperative company for joint sales; (2) The coal produced by each mine should be analyzed for its composition and use by the Coal Quality Inspection Committee to determine its grade; (3) All coal produced by the cooperative mines should be sold by the cooperative company as a sales agency. All foreign sales should be managed by the cooperative company; (4) The cooperative company should take the same industry association as the supreme authority; (5) Persons with good reputation should be elected by the same industry association as supervisors and concurrently serve as standing members of the Supervisory Committee, with the power to supervise and guide. (December 30th)

Cheng Jinfan was dispatched to the county on the 27th of last month to conduct a thorough investigation and clarified the matter. Wuxi 72

Widening of Two Streets to Be Completed Soon

After the Municipal Engineering Office actively carried out the widening of the section of the street from Nan Diaobiao to Daigouqiao, the houses in the area have been taken in accordance with the regulations. Now the street is being paved and will be completed soon. Then, bidding will be invited to contract the reconstruction of the Daigouqiao project. In addition, although a few residents opposed the widening of Xiatang Street, County Magistrate Yan insisted that it was necessary and ordered the technical office to actively handle it. It was specially proposed for discussion at the county political meeting last time, and a resolution was passed. Construction will start immediately. County Magistrate Yan issued a notice to the residents in the area, limiting them to demolish and yield voluntarily from January 1st to the end of February. Otherwise, it will be enforced. Now the residents in the area have voluntarily demolished and yielded their houses. It is estimated that the entire project will be completed by the middle of this month.

Pirates Rob Overnight Boat 73

There is usually a night boat between Sigang in Jiangyin and Beizhakou in this county, and the boatman is named Lu Furong. The boat left Sigang for Xitong the night before last. At midnight, it suddenly encountered a pirate boat near Baituqiao at the junction of Xideng. There were seven pirates on board, one of whom was armed with a firearm. The pirate got on the boat first, and the remaining pirates boarded the boat one after another and arbitrarily searched it for half an hour. After robbing, the pirates jumped back to their original boat, rowed away. After checking the losses, it was found that the shops had been robbed of 117 yuan in goods, 15,000 copper coins, and more than 200 yuan in cash, earrings, and other items from more than 30 male and female passengers. Boatman Lu Furong submitted a loss report to the county government yesterday, requesting the arrest of the pirates and legal proceedings.

Changzhou 74

Zhu Sen, a patrol officer at the Cuijiao Township Public Security Substation in Wu County, dispatched police to patrol the Houqitou area the night before last and learned that robbers were hiding in an empty house. He immediately joined forces with the security team to search the house and arrested four robbers, Gao Yubao, Chen Laosan, Yan Jinrong, and Ding Yuan. He took them to the police station for interrogation. They confessed to committing the crime and using the stolen goods. Inspector Zhu will escort the criminals to the county for trial on the 5th.

Qingjiang 75

Garrison Executes Captured Bandits

The garrison Chen Diaoyuan's 57th Division, 171st Brigade, 341st Regiment, previously received a secret report that bandits Hu Zhongguo and Shen Wenxiu were hiding in Wanjie. The regiment was requested to arrest them and bring them to justice. According to the report, the regiment sent troops to search and arrested the two bandits Hu and Shen, and seized two quick guns at the same time. After interrogation, Hu confessed to organizing a gang to rob and divide the spoils, and Shen confessed to following Hu to carry people. Hu was charged with the first paragraph of the first article of the Regulations on Punishing Bandits, and should be sentenced to death. After the approval of the General Headquarters, yesterday (2nd), the 341st Regiment bound the bandit Hu Zhongguo and executed him by shooting him outside the west gate. Shen Wenxiu was sent to the Huaiyin County Government to be sentenced for a corresponding crime.

Zhenjiang 76

Agricultural and Mining Products Exhibition Open

The Jiangsu Province Agricultural and Mining Products Exhibition Hall was established during the era of the former Agricultural and Mining Office. Over the years, a considerable amount of money has been spent. The collection of various agricultural and mining products inside is quite comprehensive. All kinds of fish specimens are particularly spectacular. However, during the era of the former Department of Industry, due to financial difficulties, the exhibition hall was closed and entrusted to the Farmers Bank for safekeeping. After Director Shen of the Department of Construction took office, considering that the various products in the hall were sealed indoors and outsiders could not view them, which was a great pity, he decided to continue to open the hall. The interior of the hall has now been completely renovated and officially opened yesterday. The viewing hours are from 8:15 AM to 12:00 PM and from 2:00 PM to 5:15 PM every day. On holidays, the morning session is closed, but the afternoon session is open as usual. It is said that the hall will continue to collect various agricultural and mining products from various places in order to make it more complete.

First District Commissioner's Office to Close at the End of the Month 77

The Supervisory Commissioner's Office of Jiangsu Province was originally established in twelve districts. Recently, the provincial government changed the area and re-divided it into nine districts, and temporarily established five districts including Nantong in Jiangbei, with the remaining districts to be dealt with later. The First District Supervisory Commissioner's Office was originally located in Zhenjiang, and the commissioner was concurrently held by County Chief Ye Zhendong. At present, the order from the Department of Civil Affairs to abolish the office has not yet been received, and it is still operating as usual. It is said that it will close at the end of this month because the newly established special district commissioner's office is scheduled to start operating in early February.

Silent Telecommunications Between Shanghai and Fujian 83

Taiqing Telegraph Remains Open

According to the Xinxin News Agency, before the Fujian Incident, the wired telegraph between Shanghai and Fujian was quite congested due to commercial relations, with daily business telegrams coming and going. Although it gradually decreased after the realization of the Fujian Incident, it was still able to maintain its original state. However, since December 29 of last year, due to the impact of the war, the wired telegraph has been interrupted. Fortunately, the Fuzhou and Xiamen radio stations and the Shanghai radio station are still reporting as usual, so the telecommunications traffic between Shanghai and Fujian can be maintained. However, in recent days, there have been very few commercial telegrams between Shanghai and Fujian.

According to the Eurasia News Agency, yesterday, news from the local transportation authorities said that the wired telegraph in the Taishun and Qingyuan areas has been open since the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau still received and sent telegrams to these two places as usual. This proves that the Fujian army has retreated to the Shouning area. However, telegrams from Shanghai to Fuzhou cannot be sent due to other problems, but this is not related to the war.

From Now on, Everything Will Be Under the Command of the Central Government

The Fujian Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, the Sanshan Guild Hall, and other organizations received a circular telegram from Chen Qixuan, the commander of the First Brigade of the Fujian Security Force, announcing his return to righteousness. At a time when strong neighbors are pressing us and the Red bandits are rampant, and the energy of the entire nation and country should be used to pacify internally and externally, I fear it is not enough, but they are using local public opinion as a pretext to seize a corner, placing the country in danger of disintegration and the people in the suffering of displacement. To speak of saving the country in this way is tantamount to wanting to destroy it together. Our brigade was originally stationed in Gejian for many years. Although we may face fire and boiling water, how could we lag behind? Our humble sincerity, we humbly ask for your consideration. Chen Qixuan, commander of the First Brigade of the Fujian Security Force, and all officers and soldiers kowtow together, East.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyan Steamer Ordered to Resume Sailing to Wenzhou 88

The First Sailing is Scheduled for the 9th of This Month

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Haiyan steamer was ordered to suspend its service after opening the Ruian and Pingyang routes, causing various ships in Nanshi to avoid it. After half a year, the Ruiping route has been temporarily shelved. The Haiyan steamer has undergone major repairs and has applied to the Ministry of Communications to resume its service. It has now received approval and is allowed to resume the Wenzhou service. The details are as follows:

Reasons for the Suspension of the Haiyan Service 89

Although the Haiyan steamer is over forty years old, it seems to have lost its qualification to sail according to regulations. However, its steel plates, machinery, and engines are better than any other seagoing vessel. Even newly built ships cannot compare. Last time, the various public organizations in Wenzhou and Yongjia telegraphed the Ministry of Communications to attack it, resulting in its suspension for more than half a year. The company sent Jiahe to sail to Wenzhou in its place.

Completion of Dock Repairs 90

The authorities of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, considering that the Haiyan steamer had an excellent hull, could not bear to abandon it. Therefore, after the suspension of the service, the shipping department discussed thoroughly repairing the ship. All the internal components and steel plates were replaced if they were not up to standard. The passenger seats were improved and the cabins were renovated. During the major repairs, the technical department of the Maritime Administration Bureau was repeatedly invited to send personnel to the ship to inspect it in order to comply with the regulations. It was not until now that the work was completed. The whole ship has been completely renewed. Even newly built seagoing vessels are not as strong and complete.

Ministry of Communications Approves Resumption of Service 91

When the Haiyan was about to be repaired, the company reported to the Ministry of Communications, requesting that it be allowed to resume the Shanghai-Wenzhou route to facilitate travel for passengers. The Haiyan steamer has extremely strong speed and can reach Wenzhou from Shanghai in only twenty-eight hours. It is the most popular among passengers on the Shanghai-Wenzhou route. After the suspension of the service, the Wenzhou community also repeatedly requested the resumption of the service. Now that the Ministry of Communications has approved that the Haiyan has been thoroughly repaired and has been inspected by the Maritime Administration Bureau and found to be qualified, it is allowed to resume service and still sail to Wenzhou.

First Sailing Scheduled for the 9th 92

After receiving the order from the Ministry, the company has been preparing for the resumption of the service for days. At this time, due to the situation in Wenzhou, passengers taking ships to Shanghai are very crowded. Therefore, it has been agreed that the service to Wenzhou will be resumed on the 9th of this month. However, the new routes to Ruian and Pingyang, which were previously planned, have been temporarily suspended due to the Fujian Incident. Passenger and freight services to Ruiping have long been suspended, and the market has been hit by military operations. The Shanghai-Wenzhou route will still be served by Haiyan and Guangji.

Despite Fierce Fighting in Zhejiang and Fujian, Flights Between Shanghai and Guangzhou Continue as Usual 93

The China National Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Guangdong line aircraft flew back to Longhua Airport at noon yesterday. In addition to passengers from Guangzhou to Fuzhou, there was only one passenger from Guangdong to Shanghai. The company's No. 11 aircraft, which is test-flying the South China line, still had not received any telegram from Yunnan yesterday, according to the company.

Financial and Military Reduction Bonds Drawn Yesterday Morning for Redemption 95

The eighth redemption of the Financial Short-Term Bonds of the Republic of China, 20th Year, and the fourteenth redemption of the Military Reduction Bonds of the Republic of China, 18th Year, were held at 10:00 AM yesterday morning in the auditorium of the Banking Association at No. 4 Hong Kong Road. Representatives in Attendance 96

Chairman's Report 97

I am very pleased that you have all come to attend and observe. The total amount of the Financial Short-Term Bonds of the Republic of China, 20th Year, issued was 80 million yuan. In addition to the first to seventh redemptions of principal and interest, this is the eighth redemption of principal and interest, with two lottery tickets drawn, each for 80,000 yuan, for a total of 160,000 yuan, which is two-tenths of the total amount of the bonds issued. Therefore, the method of drawing lottery tickets must use the same three digits at the end of the number as the winning bonds. The total amount of the Military Reduction Bonds of the Republic of China, 18th Year, issued was 50 million yuan. In addition to the first to thirteenth redemptions of principal and interest, this is the fourteenth redemption of principal and interest, with one lottery ticket drawn, for a total of 500,000 yuan, which is one percent of the total amount of the bonds issued. Therefore, the method of drawing lottery tickets still uses the same two digits at the end of the number as the winning bonds. The principal and interest of the aforementioned two types of winning bonds, the Financial Short-Term Bonds of the Republic of China, 20th Year, will be paid by the Central, China, and Communications banks, along with the interest due, from the 15th of this month; and the Military Reduction Bonds of the Republic of China, 18th Year, will be paid from the 31st of this month. No matter where, the national currency will be paid. Please ask the supervisor to check the lottery tickets and the bottom book of the lottery tickets for execution of the lottery drawing.

Winning Numbers 98

All winning numbers were checked by the chairman and verified by the supervisor to be correct, and were announced on a suspended sign. At the same time, the registrars registered them, and the supervisor added a seal to the bottom book as proof. Municipal Authorities Seek to Restore the Prosperity of Zhabei 99

Payment of Land Value Tax is Enthusiastic After Collection Begins

Other Districts are Also Preparing to Proceed

Since the land value tax in this city was levied on the 21st of last month, the Zhabei and Nanshi collection offices of the Finance Bureau have seen a very enthusiastic response from those who have gone to pay in accordance with the regulations in the past half month. At the same time, other districts are also preparing to collect the tax. The situation as expressed by the person in charge of the Finance Bureau is recorded below:

Enthusiastic Payment 100

It is said that since the land value tax in the seven districts of the north and south of this city was officially levied on the 21st of last month, citizens in each district have successively gone to the Land Bureau to verify their forms, and then transferred to the Nanshi and Zhabei collection offices to pay according to the price. In the second and third districts of Zhabei, there are more than forty cases of people paying according to the forms every day, and the situation is very enthusiastic. This is because the collection tax forms set for this land value tax collection are actually not much different from the grain tax, so the total revenue in the future should also be reduced by half compared to the initial budget, at most about 500,000 yuan. However, since the citizens are very enthusiastic about paying, there will be some increase in the city's finances.

Increased Area 101

It is also said that the area being collected this time is only the seven districts that have already been measured by the Land Bureau, which will be collected first. Other districts are being delayed because the measurement has not been completed. Now the municipal government, in order to increase the city's finances and for the sake of covering the entire area, is still planning to continue the process. Now the Land Bureau has started measuring, and once the procedures are completed, the collection can be officially started.

Reviving Zhabei 102

Also, Zhabei Baoshan Road, which is adjacent to the various roads in the eastern district of the concession, has been destroyed by fierce artillery fire and bombs since the January 28th Songhu War two years ago. Although some of the buildings have been gradually rebuilt and restored, the area above Baoshan Road is still a pile of rubble and has not been restored to this day. The prosperity of Zhabei City and the revenue of the city's finances have been greatly affected. Taking Zhabei's tax revenue as an example, the total revenue per year is always more than 25% different between before January 28th and the year after the war. This city is now working hard on the construction of the city center, and at the same time, it is paying close attention to the restoration and prosperity of Zhabei City. Therefore, in a short period of time, it will try its best to find ways to carry out the construction of the remaining sites in the war zone.

The Two Railways' Business Last Year 103

Surplus of More Than 3,010,000

Employees Receive a One-Month Bonus

According to the accounting office of the Jinghu and Huhang railways, the total surplus for the twenty-second year was more than 3,010,000 yuan. As for the bonus for the employees of the two railways in the twenty-second year, after the bureau submitted it to the Ministry of Railways in accordance with the law, it has now received a telegram from the ministry approving the payment of an end-of-year bonus to the employees equal to one month's salary.

General Affairs Department of the Customs Notifies Customs Brokers to Re-Register 110

All Licenses Not Renewed Before the End of January Will Be Invalidated

The General Affairs Department of the Jianghai Customs specially announced yesterday that all customs brokers must re-register: All customs brokers in this port and other ports, whether they are domestic or foreign merchants, must re-register. Between January 1 and 31 of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, they must pay a registration fee of two yuan with a Central Bank cashier's check. All members of the customs brokers' association must exchange their licenses through the association. This license must be exchanged at the registration counter of the General Affairs Department of this Customs. Any license that has not been exchanged before January 31 of the 23rd year will be invalidated thereafter, and the relevant firm will be regarded as unregistered. As for changes of address and cessation of business, these matters must also be reported to the registration counter of the General Affairs Department of this Customs. All firms and merchants must comply with this announcement. Special notice, Zhou Li, Deputy Tax Commissioner of the General Affairs Department.

Shen Yi's Statement on Dredging the Qiujiang River 113

Must Take Into Account the Interests of Farmers

More than fifty villagers, including Yin Fugen, from Yuansha, Lujiage area, Jiangwan District, submitted a petition through the Municipal Committee member of that district to the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, requesting that an order be issued to stop the contractor from dismantling the dikes and illegally occupying farmland, which was impeding agricultural fields, during the dredging of the Qiujiang River. This case has been reported previously. However, since the case occurred, it has not been resolved for many days. Now, according to the Municipal Committee member of that district, Gu Shanzhang, after this case was submitted to the Municipal Bureau of Public Works, he (Gu) personally presented the details to Director Shen Yi. Director Shen Yi stated that the high dikes on both banks were originally for flood prevention, and the Bureau of Public Works would never demolish them. He asked the villagers not to worry too much. As for the high soil inside the dikes on both banks, if it is necessary to take it, the Bureau of Public Works will provide a subsidy of thirty yuan per mu. It is planned to send personnel to measure the land starting from the fourth of this month in order to issue the subsidies. If any landowners in the area do not want to give up the soil, they can apply for exemption. If the soil taken is not enough, the river will be dredged more widely to deepen it. In this way, both farmland and water conservancy will be greatly facilitated, he said.

City Party Headquarters Decides to Move to the Old City Government Site 114

Since the City Government moved from its original site at Fenglin Bridge to the new building in the city center, the old site was originally intended to be allocated to the Municipal Health Bureau to establish a hospital. However, due to budget constraints and the fact that the buildings were not very suitable, this proposal was temporarily shelved. Measures for the National Coal Relief and Refund of Customs Transit Duty 115

The National Coal Relief Committee stated that the Tax Administration ordered all mining merchants to submit the original tax certificates and other documents when applying for a refund of the customs re-export tax, and that the refund would only be valid within three months after the tax was paid. It was also found that the original tax certificates of the mining merchants must be exchanged for distribution lists at any time and transported with the goods for inspection by customs checkpoints along the way. If the goods are not sold, the lists are difficult to recover. If the original tax certificates or distribution lists must be submitted within a time limit in order to obtain a tax refund, the re-export tax paid will never be refunded. Therefore, a letter was sent to the Tax Administration requesting that the usual practice be maintained or that a flexible method be adopted to alleviate the difficulties of merchants. The Administration replied, stating that in the future, when various mining companies declare goods and pay re-export taxes, the companies should immediately copy the number of the original tax certificate, the shipping manifest, the quantity of goods, the tax amount, and the date of issuance on the back of the customs re-export tax receipt. When applying for a tax refund in the future, this receipt will be submitted for verification. If it matches, the tax will be refunded in full as a matter of accommodation and consideration. It is reported that the Committee has forwarded the original text to the mining merchants for their information and implementation.

Ministry of Finance Sends Personnel to Investigate Shanghai Savings Banks 116

To Prevent the Creation of Cleverly Disguised Items

Pay Attention to Operating Methods

The Ministry of Finance of the National Government sent personnel to various banks in Shanghai in September of the 19th year to investigate their operations. Recently, the Ministry noted that an increasing number of commercial banks in this port were applying to operate savings businesses concurrently. The Ministry believes that savings business is extremely important for the livelihood of ordinary people and social finance. Although the banks operating concurrently have stipulated the separation of capital and independent accounting in their articles of association, it is necessary to send personnel to conduct on-site investigations to determine whether there are cleverly disguised items in the acceptance of various savings deposits and whether the operation of the savings is in full compliance with the approved articles of association. Therefore, the Ministry has specially dispatched Section Chief Dai Mingli, along with Section Members Qian Zhaohe and Xie Guoci, to Shanghai to handle savings at various banks in the area. They will inspect the assets and liabilities of the savings departments one by one, compile detailed reports to clarify the true situation of each bank. It is now reported that Dai and others have already gone to the banks to start the investigation.

Dongming, Changyuan, Funing, Shunyi, Pingshi, West Shandong, Sichuan This year (Year 22), war and floods have swept across several provinces in North China, affecting a vast area and a large number of victims. A month ago, the Society convened meetings of the northern and southern associations to discuss winter relief matters and fundraising methods in the disaster areas. It is now learned that the funds pledged by the various associations have not yet been fully remitted. However, as the winter solstice is approaching and relief is urgently needed, the Society has specially allocated the number already received, along with relief clothing and other relief items, to be distributed in the first batch. We must also imprint the spirit of our company's employees' patriotism and diligent service in the minds of customers. If this work can be effective, it can directly assist the company in developing its business and indirectly assist factories in production and stabilize the lives of our compatriots in the industrial sector."

Ren Jinping said, "Our efforts to promote national products are aimed at developing production, stabilizing people's livelihoods, and building national strength. However, we must also understand that Japanese goods are the hypothetical enemy of national products. Therefore, while striving to promote national products, we must persuade people not to buy Japanese goods. Furthermore, as Mr. Qisheng said, we must use a spirit of diligent service to help the company's business development and ensure that the total monthly business volume this year is compared with the total monthly business volume last year. There is special progress month by month to show the results of your efforts for the company and for national products. Not only that, but we must make further efforts to make the environment for promoting national products this year more progressive than last year. Our company was founded in November two years ago. Those who followed our company last year include the China National Products Company, the National Products Discount Market, and the Central National Products United Department Store. The opening of three major companies is a national products market. This is one impact of your efforts to promote national products on the environment and also a kind of achievement of the National Products Year. This year is the Women's National Products Year. Be sure to make the statistics of national products stores next year today increase tenfold to a hundredfold compared with last year. Mr. Wu Zhihao, the general manager of our company, is recently engaged in the establishment of the China National Products Production and Sales Joint Company. The first plan set by the company is to promote the organization of sales stores and create a national products promotion network. The company will rely on the power of the national products promotion network to promote the cooperation between production and sales, to transform the commercial organization that is harmful to the development of our country's production, and to assist the government in implementing the policy of economic control. Then, your experience and facts in promoting national products will be a powerful reference in the future. From this, you can know the value of serving national products, and you must increase your spirit of struggle by knowing its value."

Measures for Handling Airmail Without Sufficient Postage 134

According to Shanghai Post Office news, for domestic mail sent to foreign countries or mail traveling within the country, if the sender wants the mail to be delivered by airmail within the country but has not affixed sufficient postage or indicated that a certain section of the journey is to be delivered by airmail, the postage affixed will be sufficient to cover the fees for several air routes within the country, and the mail will be delivered by airmail within that air zone. The rest of the journey will be delivered by regular mail, or if it is faster to have the entire journey delivered by regular mail depending on the circumstances, the entire journey will be delivered by regular mail.

French Concession Police Department's Case Resolution Time 135

Deliver to the Court Within 24 Hours

The Shanghai Lawyers Association previously submitted a request to the President of the Court to correct the delay in the opening time of criminal cases in the Shanghai Second Special District Land Court and the occupation of lawyers' seats by police officers. Now, the French Concession Police Department's reply letter, translated as follows, is approved: Received your letter of December 22, regarding the delivery of cases to the court. The timing of the police department's delivery of cases is completely in accordance with the previously established schedule and has been communicated in a letter. The delivery schedule is now listed below:

Time of Capture Delivery to Judicial Advisor Delivery to Court

0:00 to 9:00 11:00 15:00

9:00 to 12:00 15:00 9:00 the next day

12:00 to 24:00 9:00 the next day 11:00 the next day

The events delivered to the court at 9:00 are those that occurred from 9:00 to noon the day before. These events are slightly less than those delivered to the court at 11:00, because the items delivered at 11:00 are those that occurred from noon to midnight the day before. According to the agreement, they must be delivered to the court within 24 hours, which has not been changed. Our department is now doing its best to send all cases to the Judicial Advisor's Office and then to the Court within 24 hours, etc. Approved accordingly, it is hereby ordered for your information. This order, Court President Ying Shi.

Alcohol Stamp Tax Is Not Convenient to Stop Collecting 136

Ministry of Finance Approves the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously telegraphed the Ministry of Finance to stop collecting the stamp tax on medicinal alcohol transported to the interior. The Ministry of Finance replied yesterday, stating: "Your telegram has been received. Foreign wine and alcohol are different in nature. After August 4th of last year, the customs import tax on foreign wine was increased to 80%. The taxes on foreign wine and similar products levied by various provinces have been included in the import tax, so they will no longer be collected. As for the import tax on alcohol, it has not been increased to 80%. The taxes levied by various provinces at 20 yuan per 100 jin have not been included in the customs import tax, so they are not exempt from collection. The current customs tariff is classified and listed very clearly. After comparison, it will be clear. What you mentioned in your telegram must be a misunderstanding. Alcohol is currently being planned for unified taxation. Before it is implemented, it should still be handled in accordance with the usual regulations. Your request to stop the collection should not be discussed."

Industrial Accident Incidents in December 137

According to reports from the Public Concession Police Department and the Ambulance Squad, there were a total of 23 industrial and occupational accidents in the Public Concession in December last year. Four workers were killed and 22 were injured. Among the dead, one fell from the scaffolding of a new building, one fell from the elevator shaft of a transportation ladder, one was electrocuted in a construction factory, and one was killed by an oxygen cylinder he was holding. Among those injured but not killed, two were caught in the belts of textile factories due to their loose clothing, eight fell from various places, two were injured by falling objects, one was injured by a steam pipe explosion, one was injured by molten iron from a cast iron furnace, and three were injured by the explosion of baked goods. The person who died from electrocution was an apprentice, and the reason was that an electric signboard was not properly installed, resulting in leakage.

Chang Yuting Case Declared Not Guilty 139

Chang Yuting, the manager of the Daguan Garden Bathhouse on Xinzha Road, Xizang Road, reported to the Xinzha Patrol that he had received threatening and fraudulent leaflets and letters, suspecting his nephew-in-law Zhang Xingran and bathhouse employee Luo Guangqi of being accomplices. The patrol filed a public prosecution with the First Special District Court. Unexpectedly, during the second hearing, patrol clerk Mei testified that the handwriting in the threatening leaflets appeared to be Chang's own. As a result, Judge Wu declared Zhang and Luo not guilty in court, and the patrol immediately suspected Chang of false accusation. The next day, they filed a lawsuit against Chang in the same court for false accusation. Chang's agent lawyer, Zou Yaoxian, requested the court to appoint another expert for appraisal and, on the other hand, requested that Chang be released on bail and the hearing be postponed. Judge Xiao approved. Last week's court hearing involved proof from the scholar Qi Fanniu, who believed that the handwriting in the threatening leaflets was completely different from Chang's handwriting. After debate by the patrol lawyer Wang Yaotang and Chang's hired lawyers Ye Fukan and Zou Yaoxian, it was ordered to conclude the debate. Yesterday was the date for the verdict. Chang arrived in court with lawyer Zou Yaoxian. Judge Xiao announced the verdict: Chang Yuting was not guilty. It is heard that Chang still intends to seek legal remedies for the false accusations and the untruthful private morality aspects that insulted him. Under the persuasion of his lawyer Zou Yaoxian, he may take steps to settle the lawsuit.

Judgment Main Text of Xie Fuci and Other Cases 141

Part of the embezzlement of prisoner rations is revoked

Sentenced for falsely registering official documents

Xie Fuci, the former warden of the Second Special District Prison and the second sub-warden of the First Special District, and Fan Guozhen, the accountant, were previously reported by the prosecutor of the First Special District Court on suspicion of dereliction of duty and embezzlement of prisoner rations. The case was tried by the court, and the result was a not-guilty verdict. Subsequently, because the handling prosecutor refused to accept the verdict, he filed an appeal to the Higher Second Branch Court. The verdict was issued a few days ago, and the circumstances have been recorded in the previous report. However, the recorded details of the case are slightly different. It is now known that the Higher Court carefully investigated the part of Xie and Fan's dereliction of duty and embezzlement of prisoner rations, and no facts were found. It was ruled to reject the prosecutor's appeal and still declared them not guilty. Only because they mistakenly did not record newly received prisoners at 12:00 AM on the prisoners' Four Pillars Book as the next day during their tenure, they were considered to have registered untruthful official documents and were sentenced to one year of imprisonment each. The main text of the judgment stated: The original judgment regarding the embezzlement of prisoner rations is revoked. Xie Fuci and Fan Guozhen jointly exercised official documents with untruthful registration, each sentenced to one year of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined, with two days of detention equivalent to one day of imprisonment. The rest of the appeal is rejected. It is heard that Xie and Fan are still not convinced by this judgment. After receiving the judgment, they will file a statement with the Supreme Court for a third instance appeal.

Li Chao's Concubine Accused of Embezzling Property Case 142

Postponed to the 19th for Retrial

Li Chao, from Changsha, also known as Li Xiguang, is 47 years old this year. He is a graduate of the Huangpu Military Academy and was formerly a section chief at the Nanjing General Headquarters. In March of the 20th year, when he went to Japan, he deposited all his movable property worth more than 100,000 yuan, bank deposit certificates, and real estate deeds in a safe deposit box at the Zhongnan Bank. In September of the same year, after Li returned to China, he suffered from neurological and hemiplegic diseases. He stayed in Nanjing and Suzhou for treatment, but to no avail. He then came to Shanghai and rented No. 4, Henry Lane, Henry Road, in the French Concession, for medical treatment. While ill, he handed over the safe deposit box key and seal to his concubine, Li Shijingxin, also known as Shi Xichun, for safekeeping. Later, because Li's illness gradually became serious, on the verge of danger, Li's first wife, Zhou Li, wanted to sort out the housework. She asked Shi for the key and invited her husband's uncle and brother to inspect the contents of the box at the Zhongnan Bank. All the property in the box was missing, and it was known that Shi had embezzled it. She asked Shi at home, but Shi left home without saying goodbye. Zhou then commissioned a lawyer to investigate the various banks and learned that there was a deposit of 100,000 yuan in the Citibank account under the name of Li Xi for a fixed term of one year. With Shi's embezzlement revealed, she reported to the Lao Zha Patrol on the evening of December 25 last year and sent detectives to arrest Shi at the Yangtze Hotel on Yunnan Road, who was transferred to the French Patrol. The next day, she was transferred to the Second Special District Court for further investigation. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Sun Penghai continued the trial in the Eighth Criminal Court. First, the patrol lawyer Fei Xizhen explained the patrol's investigation process. Then, the plaintiff, Li Zhou Likai, recounted the discovery of the defendant's embezzlement, but the number of properties was slightly omitted. She also hired a lawyer to file an incidental civil lawsuit to recover the occupied property. When the defendant, Li Shijingxin, was interrogated, she denied embezzlement and knew nothing about the Citibank deposit. The safe deposit box key was handed over to me by my husband for safekeeping. She also hired a lawyer for defense. As a result of the interrogation, the court ordered that the investigation of the case was still needed, so it was ordered to postpone the retrial to the morning of the 19th. The defendant was ordered to pay a bail of 50,000 yuan and report to the guarantor at any time.

Fan Silin Committed Suicide in a Hotel 145

At more than 1:00 yesterday morning, a traveler came to the New Su Hotel on Fourth Horse Road, claiming to be a local named Fan Silin, 38 years old. The waiter led him into a room. After bringing tea, he immediately closed the door tightly. Nothing happened overnight. Until more than 12:00 the next morning, the waiter went to knock on the door to ask if the room was still connected, but there was no response for a long time. He was deeply shocked and tried to open the door. He caught sight of Fan hanging himself from the iron bed frame with a belt. He immediately notified the cashier and reported it to the patrol, ordering Chinese patrol number 3118 to come and transport the body to Renji Hospital, and then transport it to the morgue for examination. The deceased was only wearing a black cloth cotton padded jacket and pants, and a velvet head rope shirt.

The County Government Issues a Notice to the Public Security to Pay Attention to Various Items 150

Since taking office, Pan Zhongjia, the magistrate of Shanghai County, has thoroughly rectified the public security of the county. Now, he has also prompted the various public security sub-bureaus to pay more attention to various items and ordered them to be followed. The prompts are recorded as follows: (1) Since the Fujian Incident, the situation has been serious, and we should pay close attention to prevention; (2) During the winter defense period, we should abide by the winter defense meeting, add guard posts, and assign patrols and sentries to pay close attention to defense, and report them to the nuclear department at any time; (3) Our county is adjacent to the urban area, and all kinds of bandits and reactionaries are easy to mix in. We should pay attention to investigating them. We should also pay attention to them at any time in remote rural areas to prevent hiding traces; (4) The ban on all kinds of poisons, such as red pills and morphine, is strict. We should pay attention to strict investigation and prohibition, and must not have any shelter; (5) Officials and police officers should be energetic during service hours. However, form is connected to spirit. Although the neatness of clothing is a form, if the clothing is not neat, it is conceivable that the spirit cannot be uplifted. Clothing should be solemn to correct customs and uplift spirit; (6) Police officers on duty, whether patrolling or guarding, have responsibilities to bear. They must first understand where the responsibility lies before they can be effective. The responsibility should be guided at any time so that they can fulfill their duties; (7) Sheltering gambling and hiding fines are the most polluting points in police affairs. This bad habit must be eliminated as much as possible to avoid leaving a pretext for people and falling into the criminal network; (8) The merits and demerits of police officers must be clearly rewarded and punished; (9) Public security personnel should be responsible for more than one end in their duties. The above points are just a summary of the main points. The situation in each sub-bureau is slightly different. If there are any incidents that should be promoted or reformed, all those who have public security responsibilities are expected to submit their opinions at any time or submit them to the meeting for discussion, so as to eliminate malpractices and benefit practice.

Secretary Li was kind enough to think of their plight, so they should implement relief in the shortest possible time. In accordance with the regulations, he has resumed his position as a lawyer. Yesterday, lawyer Jin Zhizhi sent a letter to the bar association, forwarding it to all levels of courts to restore his membership and perform his duties as a lawyer. However, the District Court has not received the documents from the High Court and cannot verify it. It has sent a reply to the Bar Association for verification.
